<div id="review_356966751" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/356966751" />
    <a title="Saly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3192922-saly"><img alt="Saly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1297592167p2/3192922.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/356966751?book_show_action=true">Jun 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Saly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Saly" href="/user/show/3192922-saly">Saly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3192922-saly?shelf=virgin-heroines">virgin-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3192922-saly?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3192922-saly?shelf=single-titles">single-titles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3192922-saly?shelf=celibate-hero">celibate-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer356966751" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6265020113296894512">SPOILERS AHEAD<br/><br/>My problem with this book was its length, there was way too much going on, so much so that I wanted the book to end already, I had enough of the drama. This is less of a review more of a recap, to serve a purpose for me, help me remember the developments because PNR series tend to get so complicated.<br/><br/>We know that Aeron the keeper of Wrath was chained by Reyes when he gave into bloodlust and was given a task by Cronus, kill Danika and her family. It was then that he met the female de</span>
  <span id="freeText6265020113296894512" style="display:none">SPOILERS AHEAD<br /><br />My problem with this book was its length, there was way too much going on, so much so that I wanted the book to end already, I had enough of the drama. This is less of a review more of a recap, to serve a purpose for me, help me remember the developments because PNR series tend to get so complicated.<br /><br />We know that Aeron the keeper of Wrath was chained by Reyes when he gave into bloodlust and was given a task by Cronus, kill Danika and her family. It was then that he met the female demon minion Legion and got her with him, treating her as his daughter, something for which he had always yearned for. Paris sacrificed Sienna to save Aeron and since then Aeron has been trying to cheer him up, finding females for him, something the sex demon needs. Honestly, I am tired of Paris’s whining already, all he does is be sad and drink.<br /><br />When he brought Legion with him he broke heavenly law and Olivia formerly a joy giver angel and newly promoted Warrior was given the task of killing him, something she couldn’t bring herself to do, instead she observed him and toyed with the idea of falling so that she could experience fun, joy. Her mentor Lysander (of the Elite Seven and Bianka’s consort), warns her what would happen if she fell, she would be in hell at the mercy of demons and would lose her immortality but she still falls and when she meets Aeron she is hysterical, her mind filled with images of demons attacking and molesting her and her body bloody. Olivia comes across as very gentle at first, she has led a sheltered life but soon she does become a more stronger and confident person. She knows Aeron has only fourteen days to live, Lysander told her she can return to heaven or someone else will kill Aeron and she wants to experience life with him. At this point of time she doesn’t love him and even ponders on this and comes to the conclusion she won’t give up her life for him.<br /><br />I had a hard time with Aeron, he wasn’t very nice at first to Olivia, even though he knew she fell for him, he is very confident that she could not have possibly killed him. He is someone quite isolated that wants to take care of friends and can’t comprehend how humans can enjoy their so short life, which he later himself experiences. He is happy taking care of Legion and Paris, he doesn’t need another person to care for but Olivia is not taking no for an answer and helping her is Camero and Kaia.<br /><br />Other developments, a bunch of them find the Unspoken One’s who are butt ugly and know where the artifacts are and pit Galen and the others to see who will kill Cronus for them. Galen on the other hand is evil as ever, managing to find the invisibility cloak (which Olivia later steals from him), and putting the demon of Distrust into one of his female soldiers. More trouble for the Lords come in the form of Scarlet, another demon possessed Titan, who houses nightmares. They learned in earlier books that the imprisoned Titans were forced to house demons and Lysander tells them Cronus has Greed and his enemy wife Rhea, Strife. Rhea is the mother of Scarlet and working with Galen and also gives them poisoned water, used as bullets against the Lords.<br />Gideon is giddy to meet nightmare and Scarlet tells him she is his wife, their book is next so let’s see how that goes.<br /><br />Legion, oh my god, I HATED her, she was so damn annoying. She loves Aeron and not as a daughter and when she tries to attack Olivia and is stopped she goes to hell where she meets Lucifer, where she does the most hateful think ever, make a deal with him. He will make her pretty and she has nine days to get Aeron in bed and if she fails Lucifer will possess her body (later she finds out he plans to kill the Lords).<br /><br />I didn’t enjoy the romance as much, it felt one-sided will Olivia doing everything, she even gave up her honest voice for him and when Galen was torturing her refused to go back to heaven because she made a promise to Aeron to tell him goodbye.<br /><br />Aeron’s demon loves Olivia and it takes him a while to give in to her, he wants her to go back and has been warned by Lysander, but when he completely falls for her he learns what Legion has done and has to help her even if it means sleeping with her.<br /><br />Legion was so hateful and I loved it when Olivia told her what love really is, it is making the other person happy, even then she doesn’t let the others know Olivia has been taken and when she sees Aeron in agony realizes her folly and goes to kill Galen.<br /><br />Aeron’s actions in the end kind of made me warm up to him a little, he died for Olivia, knowing full well he could not have betrayed her with Legion and that his death would make Lucifer’s pact void and give Olivia her wings back. Of course in the after life he meets Baden, who tells him that he allowed himself to be seduced by Haidee and killed because he was tired and Pandora is also there. He of course returns immortal but without his demon because of Olivia. His demon is in Sienna. In the end too everyone is ready to break Legion out of hell because after everything Olivia managed to bring pardon for her.<br /><br />Too goody shoes heroine who sacrifice everything for a hero I am lukewarm too, doesn't work much for me. The book seemed never ending with too much crammed in.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6265020113296894512" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_89318807" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/89318807" />
    <a title="Zeek" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2478293-zeek"><img alt="Zeek" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1339154824p2/2478293.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/89318807?book_show_action=true">Feb 11, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zeek" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zeek" href="/user/show/2478293-zeek">Zeek</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=favorites-pnr">favorites-pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer89318807" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12855583510026045174">Angelic being, Olivia, has been watching the Lords of the Underworld for some time now- one particular Lord to be specific- Aeron the keeper of the demon of Wrath. When Aeron gets into trouble with the Angelic council for aiding anther lessor demon and releasing her into the world, Olivia has no chance to save him- unless she falls. Making the ultimate sacrifice, she leaves her heavenly home and joins Aeron on earth as a mere mortal- well, a significantly diminished angel anyway. <br/><br/>Aeron is instan</span>
  <span id="freeText12855583510026045174" style="display:none">Angelic being, Olivia, has been watching the Lords of the Underworld for some time now- one particular Lord to be specific- Aeron the keeper of the demon of Wrath. When Aeron gets into trouble with the Angelic council for aiding anther lessor demon and releasing her into the world, Olivia has no chance to save him- unless she falls. Making the ultimate sacrifice, she leaves her heavenly home and joins Aeron on earth as a mere mortal- well, a significantly diminished angel anyway. <br /><br />Aeron is instantly drawn to the ethereal woman that crawls her way to the Lords’ doorstep one day, but he wants nothing to do with her and is determined to be rid of her. He has no choice, because no woman is safe around the demon he keeps inside of himself to protect the world… only the demon is strangely soothed by Olivia.<br /><br />But things get even more complicated when the little demon he’s begun to think of as a daughter makes a pact with Lucifer to win the man she loves with a very adult passion. <br /><br />Meanwhile the Lords continue to seek out the powerful artifacts that will destroy their arch nemesis and send him to hell once and for all while walking a tightrope between the aid they need from the capricious gods and keeping them at a safe distance.<br /><br />Will Aeron and Olivia submit to the passion brewing between them like both so desperately want or will both commit the ultimate sacrifice to save each other from destruction?<br /><br />Okay, a lot going on in this novel and to be honest it served as a major distraction from the potential for a passionate romance between Aeron and Olivia. There was so much going on I simply couldn’t get to know the h/h like I need to for me to really fall for book. Much of how Olivia fell in love with Aaron was relegated to back story- she watched him from the heavens for quite some time before she “fell” to be with him, and that we didn’t see, but were told about it. Still, the other stuff going on was important for the over arching story- so I can’t completely fault Showalter for wanting it in. (How this book ends is actually very important to other characters coming up!) I just wish we could have had more depth from Aeron &amp; Olivia.<br /><br />Oh and another thing that *really* bugged me, was Aeron’s little demon friend Legion. She was mean and spiteful and not likable at all… I know, I know, she’s a demon, Zeek, its in her nature, but it just made me wonder why Aeron preferred her all the time? I simply didn’t get it and in the end she just annoyed the crap out of me. ::shrug::<br /><br />So, whereas I’m decidedly less than enthusiastic about this entry into the Lords of the Underworld series, it is important to the totality of it and shouldn’t be missed.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12855583510026045174" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/155541961?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen Davis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen Davis" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis">Jen Davis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669344-jen-davis?shelf=pararnormal-romance">pararnormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669344-jen-davis?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669344-jen-davis?shelf=lords-of-the-underworld">lords-of-the-underworld</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer155541961" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2846722052688637786">I'm a sucker for a tortured hero. It's one of the reasons I loved Lucien's book so much. But Aeron... poor, poor Aeron. He always puts the needs of his loved ones first. He rarely seeks happiness for himself, because he doesn't really think he deserves it. But Olivia knows better. She is angel tasked with killing him. His crime: rescuing his beloved Legion from Hell. Olivia is given a choice... kill Aeron or lose her status as an angel. But in the weeks she has been secretly observing Aeron, she</span>
  <span id="freeText2846722052688637786" style="display:none">I'm a sucker for a tortured hero. It's one of the reasons I loved Lucien's book so much. But Aeron... poor, poor Aeron. He always puts the needs of his loved ones first. He rarely seeks happiness for himself, because he doesn't really think he deserves it. But Olivia knows better. She is angel tasked with killing him. His crime: rescuing his beloved Legion from Hell. Olivia is given a choice... kill Aeron or lose her status as an angel. But in the weeks she has been secretly observing Aeron, she has fallen in love with him. So she makes the sacrifice of becoming human to give him a reprieve and to allow her a chance to meet him. Becoming a fallen angel is excruciating. She comes to Aeron bleeding and broken. He fights the pull he feels toward her. (Don't they always?) But she is persistent in trying to win him.<br /><br />There is a lot going on in this story. Aeron is trying to protect Olivia, the other Lords, and Legion, who he sees as the daughter he never had. But Legion wants Aeron to love her in a very different way. It was creepy and disturbing to watch the lengths she goes to. We've got great advancement of the series story arc and a solid set-up for Gideon's story. There is also a fantastic surprise ending that I never saw coming.<br /><br />But as great as all that was, the very best part of the book was the absolutely amazing romance between Aeron and Olivia. It was both sweet and scorching. All hail Gena Showalter. 5 stars.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2846722052688637786" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        rated it

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67226757-courtrocks?shelf=great-paranormal-books">great-paranormal-books</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer3241162807&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3241162807" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3659408110051788102">3.5 Wrath Stars!<br/><br/>Okay, so this one I have mixed feelings on. On one hand I LOVED Aeron and Olivia, a tattoo covered demon and an angel, what's better than that? I love how even though Olivia was just fallen, she was so determined to be with Aeron, and normally I don't like when the heroine chases, but Olivia and even Anya, who both did the chasing, were pretty confident in themselves and I think it works super well for them, and it makes it a pretty enjoyable read. Especially when Olivia would ma</span>
  <span id="freeText3659408110051788102" style="display:none">3.5 Wrath Stars!<br /><br />Okay, so this one I have mixed feelings on. On one hand I LOVED Aeron and Olivia, a tattoo covered demon and an angel, what's better than that? I love how even though Olivia was just fallen, she was so determined to be with Aeron, and normally I don't like when the heroine chases, but Olivia and even Anya, who both did the chasing, were pretty confident in themselves and I think it works super well for them, and it makes it a pretty enjoyable read. Especially when Olivia would make Aeron tongue-tied when she would come onto him super strong, those were the best parts haha. I also loved Aeron, and how almost soft-hearted he is, despite what he looks like. And I think out of all the books, these two probably had some of the sweetest and most adorable moments.<br /><br />Also, Gideon and Scarlet?? I definitely need to read their book after that bomb. I feel as if so far in the series, most of the books are a bit repetitive in the romance and plot aspect. They find some special heroine, and push and pull the entire book, and then some Hunter action at the end, and that is pretty much the whole plot. But with Gideon and Scarlet I'm hoping it is something pretty different, and I'm really excited for that book. Also, I haven't read Lysander's novella, but will definitely be reading it after this.<br /><br />Now onto the things I didn't like... Which was the subplot and some of the side characters. The whole Legion subplot, I really could have done without, if anything, I think this book maybe could have been a 5 star without Legion or any scenes with her. I love how Aeron always treated her as a daughter, but I think he was definitely too sweet with her after everything she had done. And then after the bomb Legion dropped on them? I feel like he didn't even fight it, and if I was Olivia, I wouldn't even have waited for Aeron to sleep with Legion, I would have left right then, especially after it being right after they have sex for the first time, and he just accepted it too fast. And then for him to plan to still sleep with Legion up until 40 pages left in the book? Ya no. It doesn't matter to me if he wouldn't have actually been able to do it or not, he still planned to, especially knowing what it would do to Olivia. So I really could have done without all of that and Legion.<br /><br />Also, Gilly and William... Luckily i know they wont end up together, but where the F did that come from? I feel as if the author just tried to create some feelings between them for fillers and drama, because I don't know why the author would put them together at all. Gilly is WAY too immature. I know she is only a teenager, but if she continues on this way, I don't really think I will enjoy her book. Luckily though I still have several books before hers, so onto the next one!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3659408110051788102" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('x+Yod1VZMZRUtsZ9TwYZHOxfrVhbQ+BRwWGFNTFrhFzLY1oHINbXEi4/A/ZH8Uan4NYUlfCR4RdGmL3r6ZCrtw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer8930400920794326917">Gena Showalter is the New York Times and USA TODAY bestselling author of over seventy books, including the acclaimed Lords of the Underworld series, the Gods of War series, the White Rabbit Chronicles, and the Forest of Good and Evil series. She writes sizzling paranormal romance, heartwarming contemporary romance, and unputdownable young adult novels, and lives in Oklahoma City with her family an</span>
  <span id="freeText8930400920794326917" style="display:none">Gena Showalter is the New York Times and USA TODAY bestselling author of over seventy books, including the acclaimed Lords of the Underworld series, the Gods of War series, the White Rabbit Chronicles, and the Forest of Good and Evil series. She writes sizzling paranormal romance, heartwarming contemporary romance, and unputdownable young adult novels, and lives in Oklahoma City with her family and menagerie of dogs and cats. </span>
